 (= (contains $list $condition)  
  (if 
    (== $list ()) False 
    (let $head 
      (car-atom $list) 
      (if 
        ($condition $head) True 
        (let $tail 
          (cdr-atom $list) 
          (contains $tail $condition))))))

/*
```
```load
;;; Check whether atom is space comparing its type with type of the &self atom
```
```metta
*/

 (: is-space (-> Atom Bool))

/*
```
```load
```
```metta
*/

 (= (is-space $atom)  
  (let* 
    ( ($type (get-type $atom)) ($space (get-type &self))) 
    (== $type $space)))

/*
```
```load
;;; It's first atom is a space
```
```metta
*/

!(assertEqual (let $x (collapse (get-atoms &m)) (contains $x is-space)) True)
